- "We use this string to artificially limit the size of the release date string in our widget so we can show different content if it doesn't fit. It only really works for languages that have very short release date formats like English, French, and Chinese. If the language has short strings and this works well fill out this string and we will use it to decide what to show. If the language has long strings or has complex formats, leave this as an empty string and we will not attempt to size any text.\n\nThis should be the widest string in the language for the strings representing '1s-59s ago', '1m-59m ago', '1h-23h ago', and '1d-6d ago'. These are generated using Date.RelativeFormatStyle with min, hour, day allowed, .numeric presentation and .narrow units style. We default to an empty string ''. Ex: en-US has '59m ago', fr-FR could be '-59 min', zh-CN could be '59分钟前', en-UK could be '59 min ago', ar has long strings and shouldn't use this. See rdar matching for more examples."
